name:w‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äça‚Äço‚Äç8‚Äç2
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:13 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 22, 2024
msg:A perfect experience! It is definitely another top five-star hotel in Guangzhou!

Compared with five-star hotels in CBD high-rise buildings such as Rosewood, Four Seasons, Ritz-Carlton, Mandarin Oriental, and W, this place is more like a resort, a holiday paradise. The hotel is located on Haixinsha Island, the quietest place in Guangzhou. The hotel consists of a low-rise building, and the design combines modernity and age. It is very comfortable to walk inside. The distance from the parking lot to the lobby is a three-minute walk, but you can also experience the hotel's "classic car" pick-up. The infinity pool faces the Pearl River and Liede Bridge, and the East and West Towers are next to it. The large balcony in the room allows us to listen to the sound of rain and quietly watch the scenery of Guangzhou Tower. Whether it is day or night, the scenery is online!

But the biggest surprise is far more than that. The first surprise: We were attracted by a place called the bird watching platform, and curiously took the elevator to the 6th floor. It turned out that there was a different world here. We ran from the bottom of the woods to the top of the woods, and we were shocked by the scenery. This is the habitat of all kinds of birds, big and small. I didn't expect that there would be such an original ecological scene next to the downtown area of ‚Äã‚ÄãGuangzhou.

Surprise 2: This place highlights the integration of Lingnan cultural elements, which is vividly reflected in the design details and catering. As a native Guangzhou native, I love Cantonese breakfast. I didn't expect that the buffet breakfast also has Cantonese rice noodles, pork feet ginger, chicken biscuits, barbecued pork crisps, and sachima, not to mention the standard shrimp dumplings, shishimai, radish beef brisket, and wonton noodles. Shrimp dumplings and shishimai were pushed out of the teahouse cart, giving us a sense of nostalgia. Fruits also include Feizixiao lychees that have been on the market for a short time. The key to the above is that the taste is very online and authentic!

The service is meticulous, from the lobby to the executive lounge to the swimming pool, every place gives us the most intimate service. Special thanks to the duty manager Ares, the front desk Somi, Alex, you are so greatüëç

posted:Posted May 27, 2024
msg:The first time I went to Guangzhou, I encountered heavy rain in April and flights were cancelled continuously. The hotel I originally booked on Ctrip for April 20 was canceled and postponed to May 20.
The day before departure, Alex from the concierge called and added WeChat. He is a very responsible and sunny boy. You can send a message at any time if you have any questions, and he will reply as soon as possible.
The hotel is on an island called Haixinsha. The hotel was formerly a navy dormitory. The interior was renovated without changing the dormitory form. The package I bought from Ctrip at that time was a balcony view king bed room. I thought it would be great to have a balcony, but it was actually a very small corner balcony. If the next door guests were also on the balcony at the same time, they would look at each other and hold hands. At the time, the front desk checked in and said that I had upgraded the room to a Guangzhou Tower view room. I was so excited. I opened the balcony door and saw the view in Figure 1. The interior decoration of the room reveals a strong Lingnan style, which is the feeling I like. But the layout of this room is very strange. The bathroom shower room is at the innermost, and the bed can be seen when the door is opened. The sewer in the shower room is still blocked. The hotel's slippers faded badly, and my white socks turned red, and I couldn't wash them clean.
You can enjoy the view of Guangzhou Tower by walking along the river bank of the hotel. The road is not closed, so the privacy of the hotel is a bit poor, and tourists from outside can walk into the hotel area at any time. And some houses in the hotel are rented out to individuals outside. The hotel may have a good ecology, with a group of birds living there for a long time. It's a bit noisy in the morning, and you have to be careful of being hit by **** when walking under the trees.
The best view of Guangzhou Tower in the hotel may be the top floor hotel, but there is a minimum consumption.
In the off-season, the hotel organizes social hours for guests staying in the hotel, with snacks, free drinks and beverages. There are not many varieties of things, and the form is good. The service is not very enthusiastic.
The breakfast room is beautiful, with a strong Lingnan style. There are not many categories, but it has local characteristics. Before the shrimp dumplings and steamed buns, I saw netizens saying that there would be a dining car to deliver the food. I waited for a long time but didn't see the dining car, so I took the initiative to ask the service staff to take it. There weren't many people in the off-season, and the shrimp dumplings were hidden away...
Summary: If you want to enjoy the view, book the most expensive room. Otherwise, choose another one.

msg:The location of the hotel is really amazing
Facing the Canton Tower, inside Haixinsha Park, the former site of the Asian Games, surrounded by water on three sides, the ecological environment is well protected.
Yes, at first glance, it feels a bit like a resort in Chiang Mai, and also looks a bit like the Murray Hotel in Hong Kong. I thought it should be a combination of modern style and natural style. This is also consistent with the concept of "Oasis in the Heart of the Island" they promote.
But what surprised me most after arriving was the strong Lingnan style.
This time I stayed in two apar**ent types: one-bedroom suite and Xinyue Tower View Suite.
Although the two rooms are different in size, they both cleverly incorporate various Lingnan cultures.
The embroidered menu, the rich colors, the use of various lion heads, and the colorful Manchurian windows always make me feel like I have traveled to a wealthy family in Xiguan. I no longer have the illusion of pretending to be on vacation abroad. Yes, I am vacationing in the more unique Lingnan culture~ It‚Äôs very lively and romantic~
In addition, in order to highlight the holiday feeling, the hotel offers a welcome drink, a social time at the bar in the evening, and a favorite breakfast until 12 o'clock for those who like to sleep until they wake up naturally! That‚Äôs right, it‚Äôs until 12 noon~ I really hope all resort hotels in China will follow this~ It‚Äôs greatüëè
The only nitpick I wish was that the breakfast menu could be changed to the AB version every other day. After eating it for four days, there was basically no change. After two days, I got a little tired of it. The handmade shrimp dumplings that I thought were delicious were unfortunately only available on a regular basis. This is very important to me. I feel embarrassed every time I ask
In short, if you come to Guangzhou and want to see the Canton Tower, or are looking for a sense of escapism, or are interested in Lingnan style, this hotel is suitable for you.

msg:I have always been deeply impressed by Indigo‚Äôs official slogan, ‚ÄúJust as there are no two identical leaves in the world, there are no two similar Hotel Indigo in the world.‚Äù

Indigo Guangzhou is built on Haixinsha Island, located on one side of the island. It can be called a pure land in the busy city.

The first service of the hotel is to be picked up by a retro classic car, passing through an egret sanctuary and arriving at the lobby where an ancient banyan tree sits.

The check-in front desk was transformed from three dragon boat drums, echoing the Dragon Boat Festival culture of southern Guangdong.

The room layout is in the new Chinese style, with Lao Guang elements incorporated everywhere. The Manchurian windows in Lao Xiguan, the lion dance pillows in the sofa area, and the flowery carpets have a strong retro style.

The room type is equipped with a balcony, and the slim waist stands proudly in front of you.
